"\nText\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n|\n\n\n\n52013PC0056\n\nProposal for a COUNCIL DIRECTIVE adapting Directives 67/548/EEC and 1999/45/EC in the field of environment, by reason of the accession of Croatia /* COM/2013/056 final - 2013/0035 (NLE) */\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nEXPLANATORY MEMORANDUM\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 CONTEXT OF THE PROPOSAL\nThe proposal for a Council Directive adapting\nDirectives 67/548/EEC and 1999/45/EC in the field of environment is\nnecessitated by the upcoming accession of the Republic of Croatia to the\nEuropean Union.\nThe Treaty concerning the accession of the Republic of Croatia to the European Union[1]\nwas signed by all Member States of the European Union and the Republic of Croatia at Brussels on 9 December 2011.\nArticle 3 (3) of the Treaty of Accession\nprovides that it shall enter into force on 1 July 2013 provided that all the\ninstruments of ratification have been deposited before that date.\nArticle 3(4) of the Treaty of Accession of the Republic of Croatia enables the institutions of the Union to adopt before accession measures\nreferred to, inter alia, in Article 50 of the Act concerning the conditions of\naccession of the Republic of Croatia[2].\nThese measures shall enter into force only subject to and on the date of the\nentry into force of the Treaty of Accession.\nArticle 50 of the Act of Accession provides that where acts of the institutions adopted prior to\naccession require adaptation by reason of accession, and the necessary\nadaptations have not been provided for in this Act or its Annexes, the Council\nor the Commission (if the original acts were adopted by the Commission) shall\nadopt the necessary acts. \nPoint 2 of the Final Act[3] refers\nto the political agreement on a set of adaptations to be adopted by the\ninstitutions which was reached between the Member States and Croatia in the\ncontext of the approval of the Treaty of Accession; the High Contracting\nParties of the Treaty of Accession invited the Council and the Commission to\nadopt these adaptations before accession in accordance with Article 50 of the\nAct of Accession, completed and updated where necessary to take account of the\nevolution of the law of the Union.\nThe present proposal covers technical\nadaptations in the field of environment as regards firstly Directive 67/548/EEC\non the approximation of laws, regulations and administrative provisions\nrelating to the classification, packaging and labelling of dangerous\nsubstances, and secondly Directive 1999/45/EC concerning the approximation of\nthe laws, regulations and administrative provisions of the Member States\nrelating to the classification, packaging and labelling of dangerous\npreparations, by reason of the accession of Croatia. Both Directives were\nrepealed by Regulation 2008/1272/EC on classification, labelling and packaging\nof substances and mixtures, amending and repealing Directives 67/548/EEC and\n1999/45/EC and amending Regulation (EC) No 1907/2006. The validity of both Directives\n67/548/EEC and 1999/45/EC will end on 31 May 2015. Both Directives fall within\nthe field of environment \u2013 corresponding to negotiation chapter 27.\nThis proposal is part of a series of proposals\nfor Council directives by the Commission to the Council which regroup the\ntechnical adaptations to Council directives as well as to European Parliament\nand Council directives corresponding to negotiation chapters into separate\nproposals for different Council directives. This structure is designed to\nfacilitate the transposition of the directives concerned by Member States into\ntheir respective legal orders. The package of proposals for legal acts which\nthe Commission has transmitted to the Council is composed of this series of\nproposals for Council directives on the one hand, as well as of a proposal for\na single Council regulation which covers the relevant European Parliament and\nCouncil regulations and decisions as well as the relevant Council regulations\nand decisions on the other hand. This is in line with the approach which was\ntaken in the past in view of the accession of Bulgaria and Romania[4].\nIt is foreseen that all the legal acts included\nin this package will be published in the Official Journal of the European\nUnion at the same date.\nThe present proposal and the other proposals\nincluded in this package will take into account technical adaptations to the acquis\nwhich were published in the Official Journal of the European Union until 1\nSeptember 2012. The reasons for this are to provide sufficient time for the\nlegislative processes involved on the one hand, and for the fulfilment of the ensuing\ntransposition and notification obligations by Member States as regards\ndirectives on the other hand. Adaptations which may be necessary to the acquis\npublished in the Official Journal of the European Union after 1 September 2012\nwill be foreseen in the relevant acts themselves or done at a later stage\nthrough the appropriate procedure. In addition, the Commission intends to\ninformally provide a list of such legislation to Member States in early July\n2013.\n2.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 RESULTS OF CONSULTATIONS WITH THE\nINTERESTED PARTIES AND IMPACT ASSESSMENTS\nAs this proposal is of a purely technical\nnature and does not involve any political choices, consultations with\ninterested parties or impact assessments would not have made sense.\n3.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 LEGAL ELEMENTS OF THE PROPOSAL\nThe proposal is based on Article 50 of the Act\nconcerning the conditions of accession of the Republic of Croatia.\nThe principles of subsidiarity and\nproportionality are fully respected. The action of the Union is necessary under\nthe principle of subsidiarity (Article 5 (3) TEU) because it concerns technical\nadaptations to legal acts which were enacted by the Union. The proposal\nrespects the principle of proportionality (Article 5 (4) TEU) because it does\nnot go beyond what is necessary to reach the objective pursued.\n4.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 BUDGETARY IMPLICATION\nThe proposal has no budgetary implications.\n2013/0035 (NLE)\nProposal for a\nCOUNCIL DIRECTIVE\nadapting Directives 67/548/EEC and\n1999/45/EC in the field of environment, by reason of the accession of Croatia\nTHE COUNCIL OF THE EUROPEAN UNION,\nHaving regard to the Treaty on the Functioning\nof the European Union,\nHaving regard to the Treaty of Accession of\nthe Republic of Croatia, and in particular Article 3(4) thereof,\nHaving regard to the Act of Accession of\nthe Republic of Croatia, and in particular Article 50 thereof,\nHaving regard to the proposal from the\nCommission,\nWhereas:\n(1)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Pursuant to Article 50 of\nthe Act of Accession, where acts of the institutions adopted prior to accession\nrequire adaptation by reason of accession, and the necessary adaptations have\nnot been provided for in the Act of Accession or its Annexes, the Council,\nacting by qualified majority on a proposal from the Commission, shall, to this\nend, adopt the necessary acts, if the original act was not adopted by the\nCommission.\n(2)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The Final Act of the\nConference which drew up the Treaty of Accession indicated that the High\nContracting Parties had reached political agreement on a set of adaptations to\nacts adopted by the institutions required by reason of accession and invited\nthe Council and the Commission to adopt these adaptations before accession,\ncompleted and updated where necessary to take account of the evolution of the\nlaw of the Union.\n(3)\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Directives 67/548/EEC[5] and 1999/45/EC[6] should therefore be amended\naccordingly,\nHAS ADOPTED THIS DIRECTIVE:\nArticle 1\nDirectives 67/548/EEC and 1999/45/EC shall\nbe amended as set out in the Annex.\nArticle 2\n1.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Member States shall adopt\nand publish, by the date of accession of the Republic of Croatia to the\nEuropean Union at the latest, the laws, regulations and administrative\nprovisions necessary to comply with this Directive. They shall forthwith\ncommunicate to the Commission the text of those provisions.\nThey shall apply those provisions from the date\nof accession of the Republic of Croatia to the European Union.\nWhen Member States adopt those provisions, they\nshall contain a reference to this Directive or be accompanied by such a\nreference on the occasion of their official publication. Member States shall\ndetermine how such reference is to be made.\n2.\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 Member States shall\ncommunicate to the Commission the text of the main provisions of national law\nwhich they adopt in the field covered by this Directive.\nArticle 3\nThis Directive shall enter into force\nsubject to, and as from the date of the entry into force of the Treaty of\nAccession of the Republic of Croatia.\nArticle 4\nThis Directive is addressed to the Member\nStates.\nDone at Brussels, \n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 For\nthe Council\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 The\nPresident\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 administrative provisions relating to the classification,\npackaging and labelling of dangerous substances (OJ 196, 16.8.1967, p. 1):\n(a) Annex II is\nreplaced by the for\ndangerous substances and preparations\nANNEXE II\nSymboles et indications de danger des\nsubstances et pr\u00e9parations dangereuses\nPRILOG II\nGrafi\u010dki znakovi (simboli) i oznake\nupozorenja za opasne tvari i pripravke\nALLEGATO II\nSimboli e indicazioni di pericolo delle\nsostanze e preparati pericolosi\nII PIELIKUMS\nB\u012bstamo vielu un prepar\u0101tu simboli\nun indica\u0163ii de pericol\npentru substan\u0163ele \u015fi preparatele periculoase\nPR\u00cdLOHA II\nV\u00fdstra\u017en\u00e9 symboly a ozna\u010denia\nnebezpe\u010denstva pre nebezpe\u010dn\u00e9 l\u00e1tky a pr\u00edpravky\nPRILOGA II\nGrafi\u010dni znaki in napisi za opozarjanje\nna nevarnost za nevarne snovi in pripravke\nLIITE II\nvaroitusmerkit ja niiden nimet vaarallisille\naineille ja valmisteille\nBILAGA II\nFarosymboler och farobeteckningar f\u00f6r farliga\n\u00e4mnen och beredningar\n\u0417\u0430\u0431\u0435\u043b\u0435\u0436\u043a\u0430: \u0411\u0443\u043a\u0432\u0438\u0442\u0435 E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi u N \u043d\u0435 \u0441\u0430 \u0447\u0430\u0441\u0442 \u043e\u0442 \u0441\u0438\u043c\u0432\u043e\u043b\u0430.\nNota: Las letras E,\nO, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi y N no forman parte del s\u00edmbolo.\nPozn\u00e1mka: P\u00edsmenn\u00e1\nvyj\u00e1d\u0159en\u00ed E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi a N nejsou sou\u010d\u00e1st\u00ed symbolu.\nBem\u00e6rkning:\nBogstaverne E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi og N udg\u00f8r ikke en del af symbolet.\nAnmerkung: Die\nBuchstaben E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi und N sind nicht Bestandteil des\nGefahrensymbols.\nT\u00e4helepanu: t\u00e4hed E,\nO, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi ja N ei ole ohus\u00fcmboli osa.\n\u03a3\u03b7\u03bc\u03b5\u03af\u03c9\u03c3\u03b7:\n\u03a4\u03b1 \u03b3\u03c1\u03ac\u03bc\u03bc\u03b1\u03c4\u03b1 E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi\n\u03ba\u03b1\u03b9 N \u03b4\u03b5\u03bd\n\u03b1\u03c0\u03bf\u03c4\u03b5\u03bb\u03bf\u03cd\u03bd\n\u03bc\u03ad\u03c1\u03bf\u03c2 \u03c4\u03bf\u03c5\n\u03c3\u03c5\u03bc\u03b2\u03cc\u03bb\u03bf\u03c5.\nNote: The letters\nE, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi and N do not form part of the symbol.\nRemarque: Les\nlettres E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi et N ne font pas partie du symbole.\nNapomena: Slovni\nznakovi E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi i N nisu sastavni dio grafi\u010dkog\nznaka (simbola).\nNota: Le lettere E,\nO, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi e N non fanno parte del simbolo.\nPiez\u012bme:\nB\u012bstam\u012bbas apz\u012bm\u0113jums ar burtu (burtiem E, O, F, F+, T, T+,\nC, Xn, Xi un N) nav mar\u0137\u0113juma sast\u0101vda\u013ca.\nPastaba: Raid\u0117s\nE, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi ir N n\u0117ra simbolio dalis.\nMegjegyz\u00e9s: Az E, O,\nF, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi \u00e9s N bet\u0171k nem r\u00e9szei a szimb\u00f3lumnak.\nNota: L-ittri E, O,\nF, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi u N m'humiex parti mis-simbolu.\nOpmerking: De\nletters E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi en N maken geen deel uit van het gevaarsymbool.\nUwaga: litery E, O,\nF, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi oraz N nie stanowi\u0105 cz\u0119\u015bci znaku\nostrzegawczego.\nNota: As letras E,\nO, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi e N n\u00e3o fazem parte do s\u00edmbolo.\nNot\u0103: Literele\nE, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi, \u015fi N nu fac parte din simbol.\nPozn\u00e1mka: P\u00edsmen\u00e1 E,\nO, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi, a N nie s\u00fa s\u00fa\u010das\u0165ou symbolu.\nOpomba: \u010drke E,\nO, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi, in N niso del grafi\u010dnega znaka.\nHuomautus:\nVaroitusmerkkien kirjaintunnukset E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi ja N eiv\u00e4t ole\nosa varoitusmerkki\u00e4.\nAnm\u00e4rkning:\nBokst\u00e4verna E, O, F, F+, T, T+, C, Xn, Xi och N utg\u00f6r inte en del av symbolen.\nE\nBG:\n\u0415\u043a\u0441\u043f\u043b\u043e\u0437\u0438\u0432\u0435\u043d\nES: Explosivo\nCS: V\u00fdbu\u0161n\u00fd\nDA: Eksplosiv\nDE: temperat\u016broje\n(nurodo gamintojas).\nHU: Legfeljebb \u2026 oC\nh\u0151m\u00e9rs\u00e9kleten, csak az eredeti ed\u00e9nyzetben t\u00e1rolhat\u00f3 (a h\u0151m\u00e9rs\u00e9kletet\na
